      F.TOKEN AS F_TOKEN,
      F.REG_DATE AS F_REG_DATE,
 FROM kbm_goods_info G 
     WHERE G.MALL_ID = ?
        AND G.GOODS_CODE NOT LIKE 'TMP%'
        AND G.IS_HIDDEN_FL = ?
        AND (G.MALL_ID, G.GOODS_CODE) IN
        ( SELECT MALL_ID,
        GOODS_CODE FROM kbm_goods_category WHERE MALL_ID = ? AND
        CATE_TYPE = 'C' AND GOODS_CATEGORY = ?
        )
        AND G.SELLER_MEM_NO = ?
  ORDER BY
          G.REG_DATE DESC LIMIT 0, 90;
